-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `league_standings`
--

CREATE TABLE `league_standings` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `league_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `season` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `team_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `rank_position` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `played` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `won` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `drawn` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `lost` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `goals_for` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `goals_against` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `goal_difference` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `points` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `form` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `home_played` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `home_won` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `home_drawn` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `home_lost` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `away_played` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `away_won` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `away_drawn` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `away_lost` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp() ON UPDATE current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `league_top_scorers`
--

CREATE TABLE `league_top_scorers` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `league_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `season` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `player_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `rank_position` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `goals` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `assists` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `penalty_goals` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `matches_played` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `minutes_played` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp() ON UPDATE current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `lineups`
--

CREATE TABLE `lineups` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `match_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `team_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `player_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `player_name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `position` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `shirt_number` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `grid_position` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_starter` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 1
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `login_attempts`
--

CREATE TABLE `login_attempts` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `ip_address` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `user_agent` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `succeeded` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `failure_reason` varchar(120) DEFAULT NULL,
  `attempted_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 COLLATE=latin1_swedish_ci;

-- Table structure for table `markets`

  `description` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `sort_order` int(11) DEFAULT 0
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `matches`
--

CREATE TABLE `matches` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `league_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `home_team_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `away_team_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `kickoff_time` datetime NOT NULL,
  `status` enum('scheduled','live','halftime','finished','postponed','cancelled','extra_time','penalties') DEFAULT 'scheduled',
  `home_score` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `away_score` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `ht_home_score` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `ht_away_score` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `ft_home_score` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `ft_away_score` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `et_home_score` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `et_away_score` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `pen_home_score` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `pen_away_score` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `minute` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `venue` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `referee` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `api_id` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `api_source` varchar(50) DEFAULT 'api-football',
  `scraped_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp() ON UPDATE current_timestamp(),
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp(),
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp() ON UPDATE current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `match_events`
--

CREATE TABLE `match_events` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `match_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `minute` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `extra_minute` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `team_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `player_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `assist_player_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `event_type` enum('goal','own_goal','penalty','missed_penalty','yellow_card','red_card','second_yellow','substitution','var') NOT NULL,
  `detail` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `match_stats`
--

CREATE TABLE `match_stats` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `match_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `stat_type` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `home_value` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `away_value` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Table structure for table `match_votes`

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `team_follows`
--

CREATE TABLE `team_follows` (
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `team_id` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `team_name` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `team_logo` varchar(500) DEFAULT NULL,
  `league_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `league_slug` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `league_name` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `sport_slug` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `country_code` varchar(8) DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

--
-- Dumping data for table `team_follows`
--

INSERT INTO `team_follows` (`user_id`, `team_id`, `team_name`, `team_logo`, `league_id`, `league_slug`, `league_name`, `sport_slug`, `country_code`, `created_at`) VALUES

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `tips`
--

CREATE TABLE `tips` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `match_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `market_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `selection` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `odds_value` decimal(6,2) NOT NULL,
  `stake` tinyint(4) DEFAULT 1,
  `analysis` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `ai_analysis` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` enum('pending','won','lost','void','cashout') DEFAULT 'pending',
  `result` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `likes_count` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp(),
  `settled_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00'
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `tipster_challenges`
--

CREATE TABLE `tipster_challenges` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `challenger_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `opponent_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `match_id` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `stake_amount` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT 0.00,
  `status` enum('pending','active','finished','cancelled') DEFAULT 'pending',
  `winner_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `watchers` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp(),
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp() ON UPDATE current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 COLLATE=latin1_swedish_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `tipster_profiles`
--

CREATE TABLE `tipster_profiles` (
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `win_rate` decimal(5,2) DEFAULT 0.00,
  `total_tips` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `won_tips` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `lost_tips` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `pending_tips` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `avg_odds` decimal(5,2) DEFAULT 0.00,
  `roi` decimal(6,2) DEFAULT 0.00,
  `streak` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `rank_position` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `followers_count` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
  `is_pro` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `subscription_price` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp() ON UPDATE current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `tip_likes`
--

CREATE TABLE `tip_likes` (
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `tip_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `transactions`
--

CREATE TABLE `transactions` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('deposit','withdrawal','tip_donation','subscription','competition_entry','prize','refund') NOT NULL,
  `amount` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL,
  `currency` varchar(10) DEFAULT 'KES',
  `method` enum('mpesa','paypal','stripe','crypto','airtel','system') NOT NULL,
  `status` enum('pending','completed','failed','refunded','cancelled') DEFAULT 'pending',
  `reference` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `external_id` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `metadata` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin DEFAULT NULL CHECK (json_valid(`metadata`)),
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp(),
  `completed_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00'
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `users`
--

CREATE TABLE `users` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `phone` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `country_code` varchar(5) DEFAULT NULL,
  `password_hash` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `google_id` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `username` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `display_name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `avatar_url` varchar(500) DEFAULT NULL,
  `bio` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `role` enum('user','tipster','admin') DEFAULT 'user',
  `balance` decimal(12,2) DEFAULT 0.00,
  `timezone` varchar(50) DEFAULT 'UTC',
